#waitai "Landing Chamber UHV CCG1", <, 5.0e-7
#email "UHVCCG1 pressure below 5.0e-7", "Waiting 1 minute further", bouet@bnl.gov, sgiorgio@bnl.gov
l1
l1
t2
n
n

DC 6000000
